\DoxyCodeLine{00201\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00202\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Platform-\/specific\ calling\ convention\ macros.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00203\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00204\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Platforms\ should\ define\ these\ so\ that\ Vulkan\ clients\ call\ Vulkan\ commands}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00205\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ with\ the\ same\ calling\ conventions\ that\ the\ Vulkan\ implementation\ expects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00206\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00207\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ VKAPI\_ATTR\ -\/\ Placed\ before\ the\ return\ type\ in\ function\ declarations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00208\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Useful\ for\ C++11\ and\ GCC/Clang-\/style\ function\ attribute\ syntax.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00209\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ VKAPI\_CALL\ -\/\ Placed\ after\ the\ return\ type\ in\ function\ declarations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00210\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Useful\ for\ MSVC-\/style\ calling\ convention\ syntax.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00211\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ VKAPI\_PTR\ \ -\/\ Placed\ between\ the\ '('\ and\ '*'\ in\ function\ pointer\ types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00212\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00213\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Function\ declaration:\ \ VKAPI\_ATTR\ void\ VKAPI\_CALL\ vkCommand(void);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00214\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Function\ pointer\ type:\ typedef\ void\ (VKAPI\_PTR\ *PFN\_vkCommand)(void);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00215\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00216\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_WIN32)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00217\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ On\ Windows,\ Vulkan\ commands\ use\ the\ stdcall\ convention\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00218\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ VKAPI\_ATTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00219\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ VKAPI\_CALL\ \_\_stdcall}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00220\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ VKAPI\_PTR\ \ VKAPI\_CALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00221\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif\ defined(\_\_ANDROID\_\_)\ \&\&\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH)\ \&\&\ \_\_ARM\_ARCH\ <\ 7}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00222\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#error\ "{}Vulkan\ isn't\ supported\ for\ the\ 'armeabi'\ NDK\ ABI"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00223\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif\ defined(\_\_ANDROID\_\_)\ \&\&\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH)\ \&\&\ \_\_ARM\_ARCH\ >=\ 7\ \&\&\ defined(\_\_ARM\_32BIT\_STATE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00224\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ On\ Android\ 32-\/bit\ ARM\ targets,\ Vulkan\ functions\ use\ the\ "{}hardfloat"{}\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00225\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ calling\ convention,\ i.e.\ float\ parameters\ are\ passed\ in\ registers.\ This\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00226\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ is\ true\ even\ if\ the\ rest\ of\ the\ application\ passes\ floats\ on\ the\ stack,\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00227\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ as\ it\ does\ by\ default\ when\ compiling\ for\ the\ armeabi-\/v7a\ NDK\ ABI.\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00228\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ VKAPI\_ATTR\ \_\_attribute\_\_((pcs("{}aapcs-\/vfp"{})))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00229\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ VKAPI\_CALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00230\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ VKAPI\_PTR\ \ VKAPI\_ATTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00231\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00232\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ On\ other\ platforms,\ use\ the\ default\ calling\ convention\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00233\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ VKAPI\_ATTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00234\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ VKAPI\_CALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00235\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ VKAPI\_PTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00236\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00237\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00260\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ VK\_MAKE\_VERSION(major,\ minor,\ patch)\ \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00261\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ (((major)\ <<\ 22)\ |\ ((minor)\ <<\ 12)\ |\ (patch))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00262\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ VK\_VERSION\_MAJOR(version)\ ((uint32\_t)(version)\ >>\ 22)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00265\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ DEPRECATED:\ This\ define\ has\ been\ removed.\ Specific\ version\ defines\ (e.g.\ VK\_API\_VERSION\_1\_0),\ or\ the\ VK\_MAKE\_VERSION\ macro,\ should\ be\ used\ instead.\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00266\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\#define\ VK\_API\_VERSION\ VK\_MAKE\_VERSION(1,\ 0,\ 0)\ //\ Patch\ version\ should\ always\ be\ set\ to\ 0\ */}}
